Seven-Province Highway Conference Concludes 98

Hankou Dispatch: The seven-province highway conference of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang, convened by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Three Provinces, held its opening ceremony on the 2nd. Five general meetings were held until the 9th, and all proposals were discussed. Matters such as route determination, funding, construction period, jurisdiction, liaison, transportation, and protection have all been discussed and resolved. According to a participant, if implemented smoothly, it will significantly benefit military affairs, national defense, politics, and the economy. The closing ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Appeasement Commissioner's Office at 9:00 AM on the 10th. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally attended and delivered an address. Those present that day included Chief of Staff Cao Haosen, Chief Advisor Zhu Shaoliang, Secretary-General Yang Yongtai, Secretaries Luo Junqiang, Wang Zhaoquan, Yu Zhiming, Director of the Communications Department Xu Baozhong, Director of the Transportation Department Lin Xiang, and the conference's attending and observing representatives Gong Xuesui, Zhang Weihe, Zhou Jialong, Zhou Fengjiu, Chen Ticheng, Zhao Zukang, Li Shucheng, Qin Fen, Qian Shiyi, Wang Lun, Zhang Jingyu, Wang Lixing, Liu Yiyan, Yao Shilian, Xu Xingcheng, and Xu Xianwen, as well as the administrative inspectors of Henan and Anhui provinces Xu Peinan, Gao Shouheng, Sheng Shiheng, Xi Chulin, Shen Peng, Wang Shugong, Luo Jingxian, Xiang Naiqi, Zhou Junnan, Liu Bingcui, Meng Guangpeng, Chen Shikai, Hu Yuwei, Zhen Jiqiu, and Chen Bojia, totaling more than forty people. After the meeting began, Chairman Chiang delivered an address, stating that starting something is easy, but success is difficult. Now that bandit suppression is about to achieve complete success, future difficulties will be even greater than today. The fundamental method for bandit suppression is to develop transportation and organize the people. Representatives should pay attention to this point. The highway conference has now concluded, and its resolutions are generally correct. Representatives should return and strive to implement them quickly, economically, and effectively. They should do the work of two people with one person and make one dollar do the work of two dollars to achieve twice the result with half the effort. Administrative inspectors should focus on identifying and recommending talent. After Chiang's address, Qin Fen delivered a response, stating that they sincerely accept the instructions of the Commander-in-Chief and will adhere to the resolutions and strive to implement them. After the response, music was played, and the meeting adjourned. Chiang then returned to the Commander-in-Chief's headquarters. At 11:00 AM, he separately met with representatives and administrative inspectors to inquire about everything. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, he met with League of Nations experts A. Gondar, Trani, Ballegeer, Bodley, and Perley. After the conference concluded, there was a proposal for all representatives to inspect the highways in Hunan. However, Secretary-General Qin Fen, Chief Engineer Zhao Zukang of the National Economic Commission, and the representatives of Henan, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces needed to return to their provinces urgently and could not go. The representatives of Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei provinces are scheduled to accompany the Hunan representatives to Hunan for inspection on the 11th. (November 10th)

19th Route Army Actively Builds Roads 99

▲ Highway from Zhangzhou to the Provincial Capital Nearing Completion

Fuzhou Dispatch: Zhou Xingnan, Director of the 19th Route Army's Military Road Engineering Office, recently stated that the highway from Zhangzhou, via Quanzhou and Xinghua, to Fuzhou, about 500 li long, is extremely important for national defense and transportation. Since construction began in sections, with each section marked off and managed independently, the roadbed for the entire line is now 80-90% complete, and the bridge and culvert construction is about 20-30% complete. However, there are as many as 13 car companies leasing sections of the route, some with 30 li limits and others with 50 li limits, which is too fragmented. He recently came to the province to discuss completing the road plan with the Construction Department and the Highway Bureau. The entire project will be divided into two major sections: the first section from Zhangzhou Jiaomei to Huian Fengting, and the second section from Fengting to Fuzhou Xiana. The connecting routes and bridge and culvert construction for both sections will require about 1.2 million yuan (including the construction of a cable-stayed bridge from Dounan across the Longjiang River to Doubei, which is the largest project and requires 300,000 yuan).

The plan is to merge the existing 13 companies into one or two large companies to lease the two sections of the route and operate vehicles. The lessee companies will each raise some of the construction costs, which will be repaid over the years with the route's rental income. This plan has been approved by the Provincial Government and the Pacification Headquarters. Therefore, Zhou is returning to Zhangzhou to personally oversee the construction of the first section and has appointed Zhang Youren as Deputy Director of the Engineering Office, establishing a branch office in Quanzhou to be responsible for the construction of the second section. He has also hired bridge construction expert Xu Shisheng to survey the water volume of the Wulong River and engineer Guo Deqing to inspect the altitude of Xiangsi Ridge (the steepest part of the entire road, about 5 li uphill and 5 li downhill) in preparation for construction. It is estimated that it can be completed within six months. After that, ordinary commerce from the province to Zhangzhou can be reached in six hours. If war breaks out and the sea is blockaded by the enemy, this road can serve as a shortcut for transporting troops and deploying defenses inland. If extended, it can run from Zhangzhou via Zhao'an to Guangdong and from Fuzhou via Fu'ning to Zhejiang, becoming the only trunk road in the three southeastern provinces. Furthermore, after the recapture of Longyan, the highway from Zhangzhou to Longyan is also being actively constructed by the 19th Route Army Headquarters, and it is expected to be completed by the spring of next year. (November 8th)

Opening of the Baosheng Temple Ancient Artifacts Museum in Suzhou 100

Display of Tang Dynasty Sculptures and Sutra Pillars

Suzhou Dispatch: The Luohan of Baosheng Temple in Jiaozhi were sculpted by Yang Huizhi of the Tang Dynasty. Originally, there were eighteen statues, artistically wonderful and historically valuable. In the 7th year of the Republic, Gu Jiegang visited Jiao and was amazed by their exquisite craftsmanship. Five years later, he revisited Jiaozhi, but Baosheng Temple was dilapidated and the statues were half-destroyed. He and Chen Wanli took several photographs and made efforts to preserve them everywhere. Soon after, Professor Omura Seigai of Tokyo University of the Arts in Japan heard about this and rushed to China to visit Jiao and was reluctant to leave. He took 28 photographs in five days and wrote a book called "Remnants of the Tang Sculpture Wall," which contains detailed research on the Tang sculpture. The book sold for 12 Japanese yen. Omura also called them the treasures of East Asia. Only then did the Chinese people gradually pay attention to them. Subsequently, Gao Mengdan and Ren Shuyong requested the Jiangsu Provincial authorities to preserve them. After the news spread, Cai Yuanpei, Ye Gongchuo, and others visited and felt it was necessary to preserve them. They initiated a fundraising campaign, organized a committee, and rebuilt Baosheng Temple, building a new house on the original site of the Daxiong Hall as the Baosheng Temple Ancient Artifacts Museum, to house the Tang Dynasty Luohan and ancient buildings in the temple. Construction began in the 19th year of the Republic and has recently been completed. The damaged parts of the Luohan have also been repaired by famous sculptors. The museum (Tang Sculpture Luohan)

(Tang Sculpture Luohan)

(The above were all taken in the 18th year of the Republic)

is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony tomorrow (the 12th). In addition to approving the letter from the Ministry of Education's Committee for the Preservation of Tang Sculptures in Jiaozhi Baosheng Temple, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has sent telegrams to the Wu County and Kunshan County governments, each preparing two steamships and tugboats (each capable of carrying approximately 40 to 50 people; Suzhou has designated the dock that has always been used for travel to Jiaozhi, departing at 7:00 AM; Kunshan docks at the Zhengyang Bridge Liutong Dock, departing between 8:30 AM and 9:00 AM, returning on the same day) to provide proper hospitality. Furthermore, as central figures such as Cai Yuanpei, Wu Zhihui, and Yang Quan, as well as provincial government officials, will be attending, the Wu County and Kunshan County Public Security Bureaus have been telegraphed to strengthen protection. Miao Qiujie Handles Salt Monopoly Disputes 101

Seven Regulations Stipulated, Requiring Both Parties to Comply

Bengbu Dispatch: The Huai salt monopoly dispute has not been resolved for many days. Miao Qiujie, the Huaihe Salt Transport Envoy, had no choice but to take decisive action. After discussions on the 9th, seven methods for handling the dispute were agreed upon. Jin Xiangsheng, the Bengbu tax collection commissioner stationed at the Huaihe Salt Affairs Inspection Office in northern Anhui, was ordered to issue a proclamation announcing the handling methods as follows: (1) To maintain the food supply for the people, the North Salt Public Business Office should begin operations on the 10th of this month. All civilians, vendors, and salt merchants who wish to purchase more than one bag of salt can trade with the office, and no one is allowed to monopolize the business. (2) The establishment of the North Salt Public Business Office has been approved by the Minister of Finance for a six-month trial period. If any malpractices are discovered, the people should be allowed to file complaints at any time, so that the advantages and disadvantages can be reviewed at the end of the period and a decision can be made. (3) Public welfare donations and subsidies for various organizations and schools, which were previously collected and allocated by the Salt Merchants' Association (the Salt Merchants' Association collected 1.9 cents from salt transporters, allocating 0.5 cents to the Public Security Bureau, 0.5 cents to the Chamber of Commerce, 0.2 cents to schools, and 0.2 cents for temple repairs; in addition, it collected 0.5 cents from buyers, allocating 0.1 cents to the Jianghuai Middle School), will now be collected by the North Salt Public Business Office and supervised by the Salt Affairs Tax Collection Office. At the end of each month, a public announcement will be published in the newspaper, and the relevant organizations will issue receipts to the North Salt Public Business Office to receive the funds. If any organizations are missing from the list, they can report to the Tax Collection Office and receive the funds after verification. (4) The salt merchant's commission of one cent should be collected from the buyers. If there are any other demands for miscellaneous fees, the people can report to the authorities at any time. (5) Both buyers and sellers should use standard scales, which will be issued for use after being calibrated by the Tax Collection Office and will be supervised by personnel at any time to prevent unfair weighing. (6) The daily salt price will be published in the newspaper. (7) Anyone who disrupts the order, seeks personal gain, or intentionally violates the regulations will be severely punished according to law. Miao also instructed the Bengbu Salt Transporters' Association that the establishment of the North Salt Public Business Office was originally a temporary measure to help large and small transporters, maintain the food supply for the people, and ensure ample tax revenue. It has been approved by the Minister of Finance for a trial period, after which the advantages and disadvantages will be reviewed to determine whether to continue it. During this six-month trial period, all transporters should understand the intentions of the government and proceed carefully. The salt must not be mixed with impurities, the weight of the salt must not be shortchanged, and the price must be fair. Do not be greedy for temporary small gains, give people an excuse to criticize, and cause trouble for yourselves. It is hoped that if there are unscrupulous people who use the name to disrupt business, this envoy will punish them severely according to law without leniency. (November 10th)

Local News

Songjiang 102

The County Government Convenes a Rent Collection Meeting: The county government convened a rent collection meeting for the 21st year of the Republic yesterday (the 10th). Over 30 people attended, including district chiefs, agricultural representatives from each district, and representatives from various agencies such as the county party headquarters. County Magistrate Shen, who chaired the meeting, reported on the purpose of the meeting and the quality of rent collection over the past three years. He then proposed how to stipulate this year's quality. The party headquarters representative expressed the opinion that although the harvest this year was plentiful, low grain prices hurt farmers and tenant farmers should be taken into consideration. It was decided by public vote that this year's quality would be 79%, meaning that each shih of rent would actually be 7.9 dou, and the price would be converted according to the market price.

▲ Another Robbery Case in Caoging: Caoging in Punan is a coastal area where bandits frequently appear. Robbery cases have been occurring repeatedly recently. Unexpectedly, on the night before yesterday, more than ten bandits suddenly came to the home of Wang Caixing in that area, broke into the house, and searched it at will. The victim dared not say a word. As a result, clothing and jewelry worth about 600 yuan were stolen, and the bandits fled. The victim has reported the case to the authorities for investigation.

Wuxing 103

Farmers Oppose Increased Land Taxes: The land tax in Wuxing County, Zhejiang, and its surtaxes have increased over the years, exceeding more than twice the regular tax. Recently, due to the establishment of an obligatory defense corps, it was proposed to increase the mu tax by another 10 cents. Upon hearing this, farmers Zhang Guangyu and Zheng Tongguang of the county believed that it violated the Ministry of Finance's measures to limit land tax surtaxes. They immediately petitioned the Ministry of Finance and the Zhejiang Finance Department to find a way to stop it. The Ministry of Finance, because the county's land tax surtaxes already exceeded the regular tax and should be reduced, has ordered the Zhejiang Finance Department to investigate and reply. It is reported that the Finance Department also believes that the county's farmers are already burdened and it is inconvenient to increase the tax again, so it will order the Wuxing County Government to withdraw the original proposal.

Changshu 104

Elementary School Teachers' Major Petition: The county administrative meeting was originally scheduled to close at noon on the 9th. However, because the educational community of this county felt that the education funds had been in arrears for more than eight months and the administrative meeting never mentioned it, the educational community of the three districts petitioned, but there was no result. Therefore, the teachers and staff of the schools in the first district (urban area) gathered 60 to 70 people in the afternoon and went to the county administrative meeting to petition, requesting a temporary motion to pay off the old arrears of six months and stipulate that payment must be made on the 15th of each month, etc. Seeing this situation, the conference temporarily proposed a treatment measure for discussion, resulting in the determination of two measures to address both the symptoms and the root causes. For the treatment of symptoms, the Finance Bureau will issue payments on a monthly basis starting in November, and also retroactively issue one month's worth of old arrears. A committee for handling arrears will be organized. For the treatment of the root causes, the Education Bureau will base spending on actual needs and avoid false receipts and actual expenses. The Finance Bureau will allocate the educational funds collected at any time for safekeeping by the Education Bureau. However, the teachers felt that there were still no concrete measures for the current issuance of funds, and made a second petition after the meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM. After repeated persuasion by the county bureau chief and others, they finally agreed to issue one installment of new and old arrears by the 20th, and the teachers dispersed.

Wuxi 105

Robbery in a Rural Area During Winter Defense: Cao Jifu, a carpenter from Yangming Township, Shengxin Bridge, Cao Lane in the county, had some savings. At 11:00 PM the night before last, five bandits suddenly came, each holding sharp blades, iron rulers, and other weapons, broke into the house, and rushed into the bedroom, scaring the victims into silence. They ransacked the house and snatched away a pair of gold earrings from the ear of Cao Jifu's wife, causing injury. After an hour, they left, and an inventory of the losses revealed that about 200 yuan was lost.

▲ Kidnapping Case Involving Communists: After Zhu Meiji of the Anzhen Security Corps captured the bandits who kidnapped Xue Dianxiang, an elderly man from the 12th District, in the home of Qian Zixiang in Furong Mountain, he learned under county interrogation that Zixiang was using the alias Wang Ada and hiding in the French Concession of Shanghai on Danshui Road. He immediately dispatched detective team leader Xue Furui, along with an informant, to Shanghai. They encountered Qian by chance on the way and arrested him. He was then escorted to Wuxi and interrogated by the Public Security Bureau. Qian Zixiang confessed that Qian Gengshang from Beixiang was a former Communist Party member who worked hard. He had no prior knowledge of the kidnapping of Weng Zhendong, but he had served as a liaison and messenger in the Lu Zugen family kidnapping case and received 20 yuan in stolen money. He was sent to the county government for interrogation.

▲ Fire in a Shantytown Burns an Old Woman to Death: In the shantytown of Song Xueren outside the west gate, south of the Taibao Zhenxin Yarn Factory, a fire broke out after 9:00 PM the night before last due to leaving burning embers while cooking dinner, resulting in a conflagration. The wind was strong and the fire raged. Before long, it spread to neighboring houses. Fire brigades from various locations dispatched dragons to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished. A total of more than 50 thatched houses were burned down. Bian, the mother of Zhou Ruyu, a Xinxin worker, was 79 years old and was unable to escape, tragically perishing in the fire.

Zhenjiang 106

▲ Public Security Bureau Expels Lu Yinmin: The Zhenjiang Public Security Bureau discovered that Lu Yinmin from Fujian, who claimed to be the Jiangsu Opium Suppression Commissioner, and then the General Manager of the Xinghua Silver Company, was making a show everywhere, hoping to contract for business and collect certificate money. The Xinghua Silver Company had long been ordered to be sealed up by the Construction Department, but Lu Yinmin still did not know to restrain himself. When the Zhenjiang Public Security Bureau heard about it, they sent personnel to confiscate his documents and privately printed stamps, and sent police to monitor him and expel him from the country.

▲ Hiding His Young Son to Defraud His Father's Wealth: Huang Zhengqing, the young owner of the Jin Yuan Money Shop in this port, although over thirty years old, has never been engaged in honest work and only associates with bandits. He has repeatedly caused trouble, and people in society have paid attention to his actions. His father has strictly taught him, but he has ignored it. Since this year, he has been with gamblers such as Fan Chengzhang, and has often lost. Because the economic power is still in his father's hands, he cannot freely withdraw funds for his extravagance, resulting in embarrassment. The gamblers, thinking of him as a profligate son, borrowed money for him at high interest rates, reaching a total of more than 13,000 yuan. He has been forced to repay the debt by creditors for days, and he could not repay it. Because of this, he had a whimsical idea. He conspired with a close friend on the night before last at about 9:00 PM to pre-arrange with a Mr. Wang at No. 65 Xinhe Street to take his young son to his residence at No. 15 Jiuru Lane, and the nanny followed. At 10:00 PM, he reported to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau that two bandits had brought handguns to his residence and kidnapped his young son along with the nanny. After Xue, the bureau chief, interrogated him repeatedly, he stammered and there were many strange points. He promised to inquire after strict interrogation, and he was suspected of being suspicious. He immediately ordered two detectives to follow him to investigate. Fearing that his report was false, he notified all branches to search closely. Upon hearing the news, all the branches were dispatched to investigate. Until dawn, according to a secret report, the child was hidden by Huang Zhengqing at No. 65 Xinhe Street. He immediately went to search the place. Huang was also present at the scene and claimed that the child had been found and asked not to be investigated further. Chief Xue considered the case to be serious, so he brought Huang Zhengqing and the child, along with the nanny and Mr. Wang, to the bureau for interrogation. According to the confession, he owed more than 13,000 yuan due to gambling and could not repay it, so he made this deal to defraud his father of a large sum of money to pay off his debts. After hearing the confession, Chief Xue immediately transferred him to the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Director Dai ordered the police to summon the gambler Fan Chengzhang for a trial, and then detained him, waiting for the accomplices to be arrested before investigating the matter and sending them to the Security Department for punishment.

Nanjing 107

Opening of the Central Broadcasting Radio Station: The Central Broadcasting Radio Station has expanded its power and built a new station. It was completed in August of this year and tested broadcasting in September. According to reports from various places, the sound is clear and loud, far better than before. It can be clearly heard as far east as the Hawaiian Islands, as far south as New Zealand, as far west as Tibet, and as far north as Outer Mongolia. The station is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 10:00 AM on the 12th of this month.

Now, the group believes that the Zhonghua Daily's supplement in this city contained a topic called "Destroying the Religion," which contains the words "It is a pity that Father Pig has no clouds, destroying the religion, do not try to save your mother's life," which is considered to be fabricating facts, insulting Muslims, and intentionally provoking trouble like the Nanhua and Beixin newspapers. In addition to sending a letter to the newspaper questioning it, they have sent representatives to the county to petition for handling and sent letters to Muslims in Shanghai to help investigate.

▲ Inland Shipping Bureau Jointly Opens a Salt-Shaobo Route: Transportation from Shaobo to Yancheng in this county has always been difficult. Gaoyou 109

Police Squad Captures Seven Bandits: Fu, a special agent of the police squad stationed in Xiejiagzhuang, a county-administered area, reported the other day based on a report from villager Xu Jiusi that Wang Rujiang and others, residents of Majiaxia, were bandits robbing various villages. The police squad leader Xu was dispatched to lead a team to arrest them by boat. When Wang and others returned home after the robbery, the squad leader arrested Wang and the other six, seized a large boat, and found more than 100 silver dollars, tens of thousands of copper coins, three sharp blades, two pigs, and more than ten chickens and ducks, and brought them back to the team for interrogation.

▲ Grain Boat Capsizes and is Rescued: Ma Yulong, a boatman from Huaian, was loading more than 200 dan of soybeans for Qingjiang grain merchant Hu Changyou the other day to sell in You. Unexpectedly, when he was traveling in Qiaojiajian Lake in You territory, he encountered a hurricane and capsized. The An and Quan Charity Ferry immediately saw it and went to great lengths to rescue Ma Yulong and his family of nine, who were able to survive. As for the more than 200 dan of soybeans, they had drifted away with the waves, resulting in a loss of about 1,000 yuan.

Xinghua 110

Ten Copper Coins Lead to a Market Strike: Xu Ruxiang, the director of the Chengguan Public Security Bureau, because his family bought rice, and the rice shop Hou Xiangxing miscalculated ten copper coins, Xu immediately detained Ji Dingchen, the shop's employee, for interrogation and punished him by parading him through the streets with gongs and signs. This aroused the public outrage of his colleagues in the shop industry, who gathered hundreds of people, intercepted Ji halfway, and pushed the escorting police officer Chen Yuwu and others to the county chamber of commerce, requesting assistance in punishing them, and the momentum was fierce enough to cause a major change. Fortunately, Gu Lunan, the chairman of the association, persuaded them with all his might, and they dispersed late at night. The next day, the industry went on strike demanding the dismissal of Director Xu. Cheng, the county magistrate, was out in the countryside on official business, so the issue could not be resolved. On the third day, the strike continued, and there was brewing of various industries joining the strike. On the fourth day, County Magistrate Cheng returned to the city and agreed to dismiss the bureau chief. The industry then resumed business.

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes a Large Number of Enemy Goods: It was recently learned that merchants in the Xiaoshan Dongxiang Xiaosipu area had ordered a large number of enemy goods in Shanghai, which were transported by sea and landed in Nansha. ▲ A Large Number of Refugees Arrive in the Western Countryside Sandy Areas: On the afternoon of the 9th, 150 Hunan refugees, men, women, old and young, arrived in the sandy areas of the western countryside. The refugees were of mixed races and acted strangely. The residents of the sandy areas were afraid of being robbed and closed their doors to protect themselves. The township chiefs of the area felt that it was inappropriate for the refugees to stay during this winter defense period, so they rushed to the Xiyu Police Station and requested that the police escort them out of the territory. The representatives of the refugees continued to ask for supplies from house to house.

A Major Bandit is Killed in Fengyi: Wang Haishui, a major bandit in Fengyi, from YanKeng, has committed many crimes and the people who have been harmed by him are countless. He has been reported to the county and wanted for his crimes. It is now learned that the bandit was captured by the first squad of the basic corps in his original territory the other day. ▲ Major Fire in Zhongguan Road: Yan Dong, an elderly woman over 70 years old from the fifth neighborhood of Zhongguan Road Township, the first district of Zhenhai, lost her sight and accidentally started a fire while cooking rice on the evening of the 7th, causing a conflagration. The fire was fierce and could not be extinguished, lasting for three hours before it was put out. More than 50 neighboring houses were burned down, resulting in a huge loss.

Shangyu 113

County Chamber of Commerce Mediates a Loan Dispute: The Chunze Company, organized by Chen in Hengshan to raise funds, aimed to promote reclamation and develop the rural economy. It was originally a beneficial undertaking for the local people's livelihood. However, since the death of the former manager Zhu Xincai, the company's various businesses have been managed by employees Zhong Zuoqing and Jin Zhonghe. The current manager, Zhu Songsan, is too busy and does not ask about many things. The business is now focused on profit-making, and the local people have complained. Recently, the company's accounts for an 800-yuan deposit made by Qian Ailin were confusing, resulting in a dispute. At the beginning of the transaction, Liu Hongjun acted as a mediator and did not charge a mediation fee. The annual interest was set at one cent per month. After the expiration, the company allowed him to withdraw the land for conversion to repay the loan. 550 yuan of the deposit has been paid. However, due to confusing accounts, the two receipts issued were inconsistent, the interest rate was arbitrarily increased, and a mediation fee was added. The records were initially forged and then altered. The borrower refused to be deceived, so Liu Hongjun invited Liu Jiean, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, to refute them one by one. Manager Zhu Songsan admitted that he was wrong and was willing to apologize and donate 100 yuan for road repairs. This could have been settled, but Zhong Zuoqing and others felt that it was too embarrassing and submitted their resignations to the company. The manager was coerced and changed his original position, refusing to mediate. It is reported that Liu Hongjun has filed a criminal complaint for forging and altering commercial records. The trial was held on the 3rd of this month. Zhong Zuoqing and others admitted that the writing was wrong, but they hid the altered records and refused to hand them over, making it difficult to resolve the case for a while.

Letter to the Editor

Letter from the 8th District Office of Kunshan 114

Regarding the matter: I recently read the Kunshan communication in your newspaper's local correspondence column on November 9th, titled "Gambler Escapes Mid-Game and Drowns." It stated that the villagers were deeply angered and gathered at the Public Security Bureau to argue, causing great disorder. It was further stated that the district office sent personnel to mediate and disperse the crowd. Upon investigation, our district did not send anyone to mediate at that time. The information in your newspaper is presumably based on hearsay. We hereby request a correction be published. Sincerely, to the Editor, Kunshan County 8th District Office, November 9th.

Shaanxi Natives in Shanghai Reject Zhou as Head of Shaanxi Department of Education 124

The Shaanxi natives in Shanghai issued a declaration refusing Zhou to be the head of the Shaanxi Department of Education, stating that Shaanxi is unfortunate. In recent years, education has been involved in political whirlpools and storms have arisen one after another, and there has been no peace. String music has been stopped for a long time, scholars have lost their education, and the national lifeline of education is directly in a state of bankruptcy. Looking back at the cause, it is due to the fact that the person in charge of education is not suitable. If we want to correct the past malpractices and save the declining trend, we must carefully select a high-minded and pure educator who has excellent character and academic achievements, is outstanding in performance, and has no partisan background to come forward and preside. The reason is easy to understand and there is no need to repeat it. Unexpectedly, Zhou Xuechang was the head of Shaanxi Education, and I was horrified to hear the news (below omitted).

Opening Ceremony in the Morning 132

Chairman Chen Heqin reported that the meeting was opened at 10 o'clock, and the etiquette was followed. Chairman Chen Heqin gave a speech, saying that today, the China Children's Education Society is holding its third annual meeting, and it is very happy to have such a grand meeting. This society held its founding meeting at Bojue Society in West Lake, Hangzhou in July of the 18th year of the Republic of China. Only about 40 people attended, but before the founding meeting, this society already had a rudimentary form. In Nanjing, several comrades engaged in early childhood education already had a research combination. By the 19th year, the first annual meeting was held in Wuxi, and the number of attendees was higher than at the founding meeting. At that time, meetings were held and everything was discussed on the boat, and everyone was very interested. The second annual meeting was held in Shanghai because of convenient transportation, and as many as 400 people attended. This is the third annual meeting, and there are no accurate statistics on the number of attendees. As for the current situation within the society, there are more than 800 individual members and 35 group members. We are very optimistic that this annual meeting will exhibit achievements in health education, because ordinary families do not pay attention to children's health, so this society must take on the responsibility of striving to promote health. As for the progress of the society's work, there is joy on the one hand and fear on the other. What is joyful is the development of the society's affairs, and what is fearful is that the outside world has too high expectations, and our responsibilities are too heavy. On behalf of the colleagues, the speaker apologized to the guests.

▲ Ma Ketan reported on the preparations, briefly saying that the third annual meeting was originally scheduled to be held in April this year, but it was postponed due to the Shanghai war. The location of this annual meeting was decided at the previous annual meeting to be held in Nanjing, which has two meanings: ㈠ Nanjing has many new constructions, and new sights and insights can be discovered in addition to the meeting, and ㈡ Nanjing schools can provide considerate hospitality. However, in fact, the preparations were not very considerate, and I hope you will forgive me.

▲ Wu Yan Yin, representative of the Ministry of Education, gave a speech reporting on the work of the Ministry of Education in the field of children's education. The Ministry of Education has a General Education Department, which has been established for more than four years. The Second Division of the Department specializes in primary education matters. Recently, the primary school curriculum standards have been promulgated, except for the civic training standards, which are still to be sorted out. The success of this standard still depends on the support of the members of the Children's Education Society. Another thing that is being implemented is compulsory education, which has compiled the first phase of the short-term compulsory education implementation outline and distributed it to various provinces and cities, that is, to set up compulsory education experimental areas as a basis. The future work plans to stipulate the standards of various teaching tools and school tools, and still hope that members will give a lot of support. The Ministry of Education has three hopes for the Children's Education Society: ㈠ It is hoped that the society will study and research more on the misunderstandings of children's education in society, so that society can understand the meaning of child-centered education. ㈡ It is hoped that society will understand the importance of children's education. ㈢ We must find a way to save the country from the research of children's education. The members themselves are working hard in children's education, and at the same time, they must guide the comrades outside the society who are engaged in children's education to carry out together. Some people oppose child-centered education and think that it is romantic and indulgent, which is really wrong. In the Three Principles of the People, attention is paid to children's personality. Equality in civil rights is flat feet, not flat heads, so we must strive to correct general mistakes.

▲ Jin Chuzhen, representative of the Ministry of Health, gave a speech saying that the goal of this annual meeting is health education, so the Ministry of Health is very willing to join. The Ministry is very willing to do things for health education, compile various health teaching materials and tools, and health equipment, etc., and has sent staff to Europe and the United States to investigate health equipment and administration, in order to implement it after returning home. I hope you will give more advice.

▲ Huang Jianzhong, representative of Central University, gave a speech saying that I am attending the annual meeting this year and representing Zhongda to say a few words. I am here to supplement what Mr. Wu Yan Yin of the Ministry of Education said about child-centered, and education is to think for children everywhere. If the teaching materials, teaching tools, and all facilities, etc., I hope you will study and pay attention to this, and do not lose the original meaning of children's education.

▲ Hu Shuyi, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, gave a speech saying that today, I am here on behalf of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education to participate, and I have several opinions: ㈠ Your society is an academic station, and our bureau is an administrative organ. Education requires academic and administrative cooperation to progress, so our bureau hopes that your society will guide us at any time. ㈡ The progress of children's education can be divided into three aspects: 1. Family, 2. School, 3. Society. Your society seems to have put more effort into the second aspect in the past. In the future, I hope you can study more with the family and society, which is a blessing for the future of education in our country. ㈢ Children's education in the social aspect is especially important in cities.

Tomorrow Morning's Event 134

Thirteen-Mile Open Race Walk for All Chinese in Shanghai

Starting at 8:00 AM at the Intersection of Bubbling Well Road and Carter Road

One-Mile Women's Race to Be Held at the Athletic Field at 11:00 AM

The Chinese Race Walking Association, in preparation for the Shanghai International Race Walking Competition, has specially initiated a thirteen-mile open race for all Chinese in Shanghai. Simultaneously, a one-mile women's race walk will also be held. Preparations have been underway for some time, and a total of 173 men and 43 women have registered to participate. Repeated practice sessions have yielded excellent results. Details of the event have been published in various newspapers. It is now confirmed that the competition will proceed as scheduled tomorrow (the 13th) morning, rain or shine. Details are listed as follows:

▲Starting Time Participants in the men's competition must gather at the intersection of Bubbling Well Road and Carter Road by 7:30 AM tomorrow morning. Roll call will be taken at 7:45 AM, and participants will be arranged in order at 7:50 AM, setting off at 8:00 AM. The route will proceed along Great Western Road, Avenue Petain, and Route Hobbema (detailed route to be seen in the map) to the Chinese Athletic Field on Route des Peres, then circling the track once to finish. The total distance is thirteen miles.

▲Information for Women's Race Participants The one-mile women's race will be held on the athletic field, circling the track four times plus ten meters. Participants must arrive at the field before 10:30 AM. Roll call will be taken at 10:45 AM, and the race will start at 11:00 AM. Awards will be presented at 11:30 AM.

▲Information for Pacers Due to the large number of participants in the men's race, it is difficult for all pacers to accompany them at the same time. Therefore, they will join in sections. Pacers for numbers 1 to 100 should wait at the intersection of Avenue Petain and Yu Yuen Road, in front of the Zhaofeng Garden. Pacers for numbers 101 to 173 should join at the intersection of Great Western Road and Avenue Petain, i.e., the Wujiaochang area. However, no further pacers may join after the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Route des Peres.

▲Competition Regulations The association considers the regulations for participants and pacers during the competition to be very important and has listed them below:

(A) Information for Participants: ㈠ Participants must proceed along the designated road and are not allowed to step onto the sidewalk. ㈠ When overtaking another participant, a participant must maintain a distance of three steps to the left or right before proceeding. ㈠ If a participant needs to leave the designated route due to other reasons during the competition, they must return to the original spot before proceeding. ㈠ Participants must keep their chests straight and swing their arms freely. They must use their heels and toes when striding. The front heel must touch the ground before the back toe is lifted, and the knee must be straight when the front foot touches the ground (it must be straight except when the back foot is lifted). ㈠ Participants who violate the above rules will be warned by the mid-course referee with a spin. After the third warning, their eligibility for the competition will be revoked.

(B) Information for Pacers: ㈠ Join and exit pacing at the designated locations. ㈠ Pacers may use bicycles or walk. ㈠ Pacers must follow only the designated participant and not others. ㈠ Pacers are not allowed to touch the participant, except to provide food and drink. ㈠ When a participant behind is overtaking, the pacer in front must not intentionally obstruct. ㈠ Violation of the above rules will result in a warning from the mid-course referee or disqualification from pacing.

▲Arrangements Along the Route At every mile along the entire course, Boy Scouts will hold a flag with the mile number written on it. Boy Scouts will also be stationed at the turns to help participants identify the route and compete. This work will be undertaken by Boy Scouts and Girl Scouts throughout Shanghai. In addition to police officers from the Municipal Police Bureau along the route and within the athletic field, the British and French Concessions will dispatch officers to maintain order. The badges for the staff hired by the association can be collected from Mr. Lu Yutian on the morning of the event.

▲Attention Referees The association convened a mid-course referee meeting last night. Attendees included Zhang Zao Cai, Zhou Yu Yu, Shi Jin Sheng, Chen Ji Xiang, and over twenty others. The chairman was Shi You Hui, and the recorder was Lu Tian. The chairman stated that in the previous event, there were stretches where there were no referees at all, and at times they gathered in one place, which was regrettable. Therefore, it was unanimously decided that this time, the entire course would be divided into three sections. The first section, from the starting point to the intersection of Avenue Petain and Route Hobbema, will be overseen by Zhou Yu Yu, Zhang Ju Sheng, Hu You Cheng, Yao Guang Hai, Cao Jin Zhang, Yu Zi Chen, Chen Yu Ze, Chen Shao, Wang Jin Kui, Cai Song Yan, Shi Shi, and Sheng Yu Du. The second section, from Zhoujiaqiao on Avenue Petain to Nanyang University on Avenue Haig, will be overseen by Zhang Zao Cai, Qu Rong Qing, Yang Pei Sheng, Chen Ji Xiang, Zhu Shun Da, Hu Bo Rong, Huang Sheng Bai, Shen Bai Gui, Yao Wen Hui, Chen Niu Tie, Wang De Ming, and Shao Le Ping. The third section, from Nanyang University to Route des Peres, will be the responsibility of Shi Jin Sheng, Mao Hong Fa, Wang Fu Dan, Yao Ming Ru, Xiao Pei, Qiao Yi Zhai, Lu Xiang Gan, Lu Zong Jia, Wang Jian Zhang, Zhang Gong Qi, and You Zhao Xiang, to ensure thoroughness and impartiality. Furthermore, mid-course referees are requested to gather at the intersection of Tongfu Road and Xiejiao Road at 7:15 AM on the day of the event to arrange for referee vehicles. They should also collect route maps from Lu Yutian, it was said.

Commercial News

Finance 137

The Gold Market is Confusing and Unpredictable

Good News at the End, Up 3.4 Taels Yesterday's market fluctuated drastically, making it difficult to predict. Industry players were bewildered, and supply and demand varied greatly, with a daily difference of 7.4 taels. However, the number of mid-term speculators remained low. The final increase of 3.4 taels did not affect the silver market, which initially declined due to the unchanged forward silver price. The sharp rise in US cotton also had an impact. Subsequently, foreign exchange trends diverged, with the British pound rising and the US dollar remaining stable. Active buying in the market led to soaring prices, reaching above 750 taels before slightly declining at the end. The complexity of the situation was unexpected. The Central Bank bought 105 cash bars at 52 taels, sold by Da De Cheng. Qian Chang Xiang transferred 28 bars to the bullish Tong Feng Heng at a discount of 7.5 fen in November, lower than before. Details of the day are recorded below:

▲Morning Opening Down 2.9 Taels In early trading, the December opening price dropped 2.9 taels to 746.8 taels due to the near-soft, far-hard silver market. After fluctuating a few cents, Qian Chang Xiang, Yuan Mao Yong, Hong Kang Yong, Bing Xing, and others sold short-term British gold at 8.75 and 8.125. HSBC sold 120,000 pounds to Hua Bi and others, causing the gold price to drop to 6.3 taels. Heng Yu and others bought in, and Citibank absorbed January at 30 yuan, also buying British gold at 8.125, causing the price to rise 2 taels to 8.2 taels at 9:30 AM. HSBC announced that the British gold was up 0.125 and the US dollar was unchanged due to exchange rate arbitrage. However, Fu Yu, Yuan Tai, and Zhao Feng Chang sold out, bringing the price down to 6.88 taels by 9:50 AM. Later, HSBC absorbed January US dollars at 9.375 and British gold at 8.75, with Heng Yu and retail investors also buying in, gradually raising the price by more than 2 taels. Speculators only made a few cents until 10:30 AM, reaching 9.3 taels. Zhi Feng Yong and other gold firms sold out, causing a drop of 1.5 taels to 7.8 taels. At this point, Yi Feng Yong and retail short sellers bought in, and the Bank of China absorbed February at 30 yuan, with Mei Feng doing exchange rate arbitrage at 3.2825 yuan, pushing the price up to 9.6 taels. After 11:20 AM, Fu Yu and others tended to sell out, and Hua Bi released January US dollars at 9.375, causing the price to plunge more than 2 taels. However, the number of speculators was very small. By noon, the price closed at 6.8 taels.

▲Afternoon Market Sharply Bullish The afternoon market opened flat at 6.8 taels. Subsequently, Yuan Chun and Yuan Xing Yong bought in, and various firms rushed to buy US dollars at 9.375 for January, reaching 9.7 taels by 2:45 PM. Suddenly, Yuan Mao Yong and Tong Tai Chang sold out, causing a drop of 1.1 taels to 8.6 taels. At 3:00 PM, buying sentiment was very strong, with Fu Chang, Heng Yu, Zhao Feng Chang, Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, etc., competing to buy. The December US dollar was traded at 8.125, further boosting the market, reaching 52.5 taels at 3:15 PM. After a short period, Yuan Mao Yong, Yuan Heng, and Heng Yu sold, suppressing the price by 1.5 taels, but there was no major change. Until 4:00 PM, the price was 51 taels, then it became bullish again because the February US dollar was traded at 8.75, and December was being pushed to 7.5. It was also reported that the Central Bank was buying 105 cash bars, causing Da De Cheng, Zhi Feng Yong, and Yi Feng and others to compete to buy, causing an instantaneous increase of more than 2 taels to 53.7 taels at 4:20 PM, exceeding yesterday's highest price. Unexpectedly, Dalian Bang took the opportunity to sell, and the February US dollar was traded at 9.375, causing a drop of 1 tael to 52.7 taels. By the 4:30 PM close, the price was 3.1 taels, up 3.4 taels from the 10th (the third consecutive day of gains). After the close, Heng Yu and Wan Xing followed suit, causing a setback in confidence and a drop to just over 51 taels, making it difficult to predict. The daily maximum was 53.7 taels, and the minimum was 46.3 taels, a difference of 7.4 taels. Therefore, the Gold Exchange has a double settlement price, and the bare bar only increased by 10 taels and 0.025 because the swap had narrowed.

▲Disclosure Price Reduced Again The disclosure price remained at 814 taels due to the unchanged US exchange rate, a pledge of 66-67 taels. Later, 64 taels, 67 taels at noon, then only 60 taels, and finally 61.2 taels, 3 taels less than the previous day. The accounting was 49 taels and 47 taels in the morning, 55 taels and 53 taels in the afternoon, and 47 taels for water replenishment in the afternoon, 53 taels.

▲Various Firms Buying and Selling Frequently There was considerable trading on the table, with industry players buying and selling. Statistics show that Heng Yu, Zhao Feng Chang, Yuan Xing Yong, Da Xing Yong, Fu Yu, and Yuan Heng all bought in. Zhi Feng Yong, Qian Chang Xiang, Bing Xing, Yong Feng, Fu Tai Heng, Yuan Tai, and Hong Kang Yong all sold out. Yuan Mao Yong hedged 300-400 bars. Da De Cheng hedged and sold. Tong Tai Chang, Shun Li, Fu Xing Yong, and Yuan Chun and Wan Xing's deposits and withdrawals were mixed, but the numbers were not large. In the afternoon, Fu Chang, Zhao Feng Chang, Zhi Feng Yong, Fu Yu, Yong Feng, Fu Tai Heng, Bing Xing, Da De Cheng, Heng Chang Yong, Shun Li, and Yuan Chun and Ri Chang all bought in. Wan Xing, Tong Tai Chang, and Yi Feng Yong sold out. Yuan Tai, Yuan Mao Yong, Yuan Heng, and Chun Yuan Yong bought and sold. Heng Yu bought in first and then sold out, in large numbers. Dalian Bang sold a total of more than 500 bars and bought more than 300 bars. (Guang Bang (Heng Xing) observed the market in the morning and sold a little more than 200 bars in the afternoon. (Yi Feng) had a small number of deposits and withdrawals in the morning and bought 300 bars in the afternoon. The number of bars at each firm was slightly higher than before, approximately 29,000.

Foreign Exchange With Slight Twists and Turns 138

Although the silver market contracted yesterday, exchange rates continued to fall. However, the trend of Shanghai exchange rates diverged. HSBC's listed British gold rose by 0.125, and the US dollar suddenly changed. The remaining Hong Kong and Dutch exchanges remained unchanged, while others declined. The domestic market was initially flat but then rose, then fell again at noon, and was very bullish in the afternoon. Although the appetite in Bianyuanfang is moving, it is only slightly.

▲In North Shanghai, the source of supply from various merchants was about 60 numbers yesterday. Transactions between the city and the countryside are becoming sluggish daily. The opening prices of Wuxi and Changzhou rice were reduced by two or three jiao for early and late rice, and one jiao for Bianyuan, etc.

Hunan and Jiangxi Rice Continues to Arrive at 2,000 Bags 154

丨Fujian Merchants Revive Procurement丨

Yesterday, the market conditions for foreign客秈rice were sluggish, and prices continued to weaken. The appetite in Benjie Street was completely stagnant. 客帮 merchants had some appetite, but ultimately hesitated due to the high prices. After the recent weakening of market prices, there is a renewed trend of activity. Yesterday, a Fuzhou merchant purchased 500 bags of Hunan machine-milled Jing rice for 8 yuan, 4 jiao and 4 fen, which is about half a yuan lower than the highest price in previous days. A Beiyang merchant tentatively purchased 100 bags of small絞rice for 7 yuan and 7 jiao, which is one jiao lower than the previous day. However, the recent客化is sluggish and prices have fallen. The Hunan rice that arrived a few days ago has not yet been sold through. After the arrival of another batch yesterday, the accumulation of inventory in the market is gradually increasing. A large amount of客化is needed for a gradual increase in prices to materialize.

Flour Market Falls Back After Being Lively 155

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, prices for each month rose slightly by one or two jiao due to slightly better quotations for foreign wheat. Moreover, because the factories were unwilling to release inventory, market sentiment became lively after the opening. Due to the rejection by major factories, the current month was not released. For longer-term contracts, foreign customers and speculators in the market bought briskly. Short sellers also took the opportunity to cover their positions. Therefore, the opening prices for each contract rose by one or two fen compared to the previous day. March was the fastest rising, due to more active buying by outside parties. By the afternoon opening, market sentiment for November and December was still stable, but for longer-term contracts, prices gradually fell back. It was heard that Fuxin had begun selling, with approximately 100,000 bags being sold. The prices for Australian wheat were low. It was heard that local factories had jointly booked another ship, priced at only 3 taels, 4 qian and 5 fen and a half (or a rumored 4 qian and a half). Given this situation, there is still a surplus overseas, and it is likely that this is only a temporary excitement. As a result, November and December were better by 7.5 li, January was better by 5 li, February was better by 7.5 li, and March was better by 2.5 li.

Wheat Market Remains Relatively Stable 156

丨Another Ship of Australian Wheat Booked丨

Yesterday's wheat futures market was generally stable. With foreign wheat quotations slightly better by about one or two jiao, people generally believed that the market had very few chips, and physical goods were never locked in. Therefore, outside customers generally believed that scarce goods were valuable, and their thinking was firm. They were unaware that the prices for Australian wheat were becoming cheaper step by step. If the prices were raised excessively, the subsequent reaction would be unthinkable. For example, the Australian wheat that was set yesterday was heard to be only 3 taels, 4 qian and 5 fen and a half. After removing the upgrades and converting to the standard, there would be a profit. Therefore, amid the falling world prices, it is best to follow the trend. As a result, November was better by 1 fen, February was better by 3 fen, March was better by 2 fen, and there were no other gains or losses. The spot wheat market was quiet due to both arrivals and sales being inactive, and there were no speculative trades.

Free Talk

Aphorisms of Ma Xiangbo, a 93-year-old

The Pioneer of Catholicism in Korea Was Chinese 171

— Jing Ji

On Christmas Day of 1794 (i.e., the 59th year of the Qianlong reign), how many Korean believers joyfully waited at the border for the arrival of Korea's first priest? In the dim twilight, a disguised Korean indeed arrived. His attire included a bamboo hat and straw sandals. His hairstyle and clothing were just like those of a native Korean. However, he was born in Changshu, Jiangsu, with the surname Zhou and the given name Jacob! The pioneer of Catholicism in Korea was Chinese!

Priest Zhou learned the Korean language and founded the Mingdao Society. He also translated books on doctrine, preaching with the attitude of a scholar. Within six years, he gained six thousand believers! He got along very well with the locals. However, this good priest ultimately "sacrificed himself for righteousness."

Unfortunately, it coincided with the death of King Jeongjo of Korea, and powerful ministers seized power, destroying the church! Priest Zhou originally planned to return to China, seeking refuge at the border between China and Korea. However, he received a divine revelation to return to the capital via the same route.

One day, at the third crow of the rooster, a person in plain clothes with a silk fan, his beard and hair neatly arranged, arrived at the prison and confessed: "I am the Chinese priest Zhou Jacob, whom you have been searching for throughout the country. I came to Korea for no other reason than to preach the Holy Catholic Church and save the souls of the entire nation! Now I have come to surrender myself." The interrogating official sentenced him to death! Later, the Korean king apologized to the Chinese court.

In 1801 (i.e., the 6th year of the Jiaqing reign), at 4:00 PM, the execution was carried out. The weather suddenly changed, with thunder and lightning crisscrossing the sky. The audience at the execution ground was extremely terrified. However, the one being sacrificed, Korea's first priest, calmly faced his death, saying to the audience:

"I am dying today for preaching the Holy Catholic Church. I forewarn the public: in the future, Korea will face great disasters. Only then will Koreans remember me!"

(Note) The "Korean Martyrdom Record" published by the Shanghai Tushanwan Printing House is available for reference.

Easy to Get on Stage, Difficult to Get off 172

— Jin Butong

丨View the affairs of the world as such丨

The Japanese army spent two days annexing my three northeastern provinces, without even breaking a sweat, as easy as pie. Then, General Ma Zhanshan rose up in resistance, followed by volunteer armies, self-defense forces, national salvation armies, national defense armies, and countless unnamed armies, launching attacks on weak points and avoiding strong ones, making feints to the east and attacking in the west, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, leaving the Japanese and puppet troops overwhelmed. In Japan, they originally thought they had single-handedly created a puppet regime, and the situation was set, but who knew it would end up like this. Their Foreign Minister Shidehara said: "Annexing Manchuria is like swallowing a bomb." This statement is

Absolutely correct. Now, because of the Japanese invasion of my Northeast, the domestic economy is in a state of panic, and the dissatisfaction of the great powers is deepening day by day. However, due to concerns about face, Japan cannot easily give up. Although the future is full of dangers, they have no choice but to persevere. This situation perfectly matches an old saying, "Easy to get on stage, difficult to get off."

Because of this situation, I was reminded of the issue of education. After graduating from elementary school, one has to borrow money to enter middle school. After graduating from middle school, one has to borrow money to enter university. After graduating from university, one has to borrow money to study abroad. Knowing that climbing up level by level through debt may not guarantee a promising future, but having arrived at an awkward situation, one has no choice. This is also "Easy to get on stage, difficult to get off." Getting to be of marriageable age, one has to marry a wife. After marrying a wife, expenses increase day by day, and creditors become more pressing day by day. Logically, only returning to the life of a bachelor is a solution, but due to face, one has no choice but to endure the pain and persevere. Only when it becomes impossible to maintain, one has to sell land and property. Regarding the wife who extorts rice and oil from him, he still refuses to give up and perseveres with a stiff upper lip. This is also "Easy to get on stage, difficult to get off." All affairs in the world should be viewed as such.

Listen! To the Words of a Japanese Woman 173

— Xiao Fang

丨I don't believe you are completely unmoved丨

It was a late autumn day, but Shanghai has no seasons丨

The San You Industrial Society was full of people, clearly all our compatriots. The shop assistants were busily attending to each customer.

Suddenly, a middle-aged Japanese woman, leading a twelve- or thirteen-year-old child, appeared in the crowd. Astonishment crept into the hearts of every compatriot: "The Japanese are the most patriotic people, how come she is running into our national goods company to buy our things?" Thus, countless gazes fell upon her.

The woman opened her mouth, speaking in our Great Republic of China's language:

"Sir丨 Please select the most durable and beautiful fabrics, those that your compatriots like the most, and show them to me丨"

The child, with a resentful look, followed behind the woman:

"Mother! Have you forgotten that you are a citizen of Great Japan? How can you buy Chinese goods?丨 Are you my mother?···" Flames flickered in the child's eyes.

"No丨 Child丨" The woman turned her head and said softly: "I am not buying Chinese fabrics to make my own clothes丨 I want to take the fabrics that Chinese people like and send them back so that our compatriots can manufacture them in the same way, and then sell them back to the Chinese. You must know: child丨 If our goods can only supply our own compatriots and we don't think about catering to other people's psychology to promote them more, there is no hope for development, child丨 I know: I am a part of Great Japan, my blood is the property of Great Japan, and I still want to pass this property down to my descendants. Child丨 How could I forget my origins? Otherwise, would I still be worthy of being your mother?······"

The child smiled slightly, but our compatriots silently fell into despondency.

— Fan Yanqiao

Today is the Premier's Birthday 175

A Commemorative Meeting is Held

Factories Operate as Usual Without Double Pay

All Government Offices and Schools Operate as Usual

Today is the birthday of the Kuomintang Premier. Due to the current national crisis, the central government has ordered that there be no extravagance. All factories, schools, and government offices will operate as usual.

▲ Holding a Commemorative Event: The Municipal Party Headquarters will hold a commemorative meeting at 9:00 AM in the main auditorium on the third floor of the headquarters on Lin Yin Road, Ximen. All groups were notified the day before to send representatives to participate. The ceremony will be very simple, with only a report from the chairman and speeches from various sectors.

▲ No Holiday: The Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau jointly issued a notice yesterday, stating that they were issuing a joint notice regarding a telegram from the Central Propaganda Committee last month, which stated: "Upon the instructions of the Central Standing Committee, the Premier Wen Jing's birthday commemoration this November, due to the national crisis, should be handled in accordance with the National Day commemoration this year," etc. It was found that the National Day commemoration this year was previously instructed by the Central Executive Committee via telegram that, due to the national crisis, there would be no holiday, which is different from regular holidays. Factories will operate as usual and will not pay double pay. It is hereby ordered that all subordinates comply accordingly, etc. This committee and bureau have jointly issued a notice on record. Following the above, it is hereby jointly announced in the newspaper that, for the Premier's birthday on the 12th of this month, during this national crisis, we should abide by the will of the central government and follow the precedent by not taking a holiday. Factories will operate as usual without double pay. All factories and laborers in this city should comply accordingly and not violate it. This is a special notice.

▲ Operating as Usual: The municipal government issued an order to its subordinates, stating: "Regarding compliance with the order, a telegram from the Executive Yuan stated: "The ceremony for this year's Premier's birthday commemoration, during this national crisis, has been stipulated by the central government to be handled in accordance with the National Day commemoration this year, without a holiday and without convening a mass rally. However, the senior party headquarters in each region must convene representatives from various government offices to hold a commemorative meeting." It is hereby urgently requested that all subordinates comply accordingly, etc. In addition to issuing separate orders, it is hereby ordered that the bureau comply and forward the order to all subordinates to comply with this order."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company 176

Four Warehouses Pledged to an American Merchant

China General Business Company Accepts the Mortgage

A Total of 10 Million Silver Dollars Mortgaged

The Warehouses Affairs Section Was Renamed Yesterday

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which the government has resolved to nationalize, suddenly experienced a major incident yesterday. The company's General Manager, Li Guojie, agreed with the China General Business Company on Sichuan Road in this city to borrow 10 million silver dollars and hand over the company's four warehouses, namely the Zong, Hua, Bei, and Xin, to the company for continued operation. The transfer was completed yesterday afternoon. There was a dispute over the transfer before, but by the afternoon, the China General Business Company had sent personnel to carry out the transfer. The details of this case are summarized below.

▲ The Loan Process: Since Li Guojie became the General Manager, he has felt that the company's finances are extremely tight. From time to time, certain financial groups have expressed their intention to invest. After consulting with Li, it was decided to mortgage the Hua, Bei, Xin, and Zong warehouses for 10 million silver dollars (some say 15 million silver dollars) and hand over the four warehouses to the financial group for management and continued operation. The draft agreement was signed in September of this year.

▲ Contract Suddenly Signed: The Executive Yuan's 75th meeting recently resolved that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company would continue to be operated by the government and planned to prepare funds to redeem the shares held by merchants. After this news spread, Li, believing that the company's remaining assets could still be freely disposed of, signed a loan agreement with the American China General Business Company this week, using the four warehouses as collateral. The company's personnel are well aware of this case. The contents of the contract are extremely confidential, and outsiders have no way of finding out.

▲ Unsuccessful Transfer: On the afternoon of the 9th, General Manager Li sent the company's staff member Wang Yunzhang, along with four foreigners sent by the creditor, to the manager's office of the four warehouses in Hongkou to take over the four docks from Manager Ling Jingshan. Wang presented the official document from the company ordering the handover and ordered Ling to sign it. The four foreigners were waiting to take over, but Ling refused to hand over the docks because he had not received an order from the ministry, and he firmly refused. The transfer was unsuccessful.

▲ Changing the Warehouse Manager: After this refusal, Ling took a half-month leave. Li then appointed Yang Ruinian as the warehouse manager of the four warehouses. On the 10th, Yang went to the four warehouses to take over, but Ling also refused to hand over the position. It was not until the morning of the 11th that Ling Jingshan left the warehouses. Yang Ruinian then took office as the manager of the four warehouses at noon, but the foreigners who were to take over the mortgage did not go to take over either.

▲ Telegram to the Ministry to Stop: Ling Jingshan first reported to the new General Manager Liu Hongsun, who ordered him to report the details to the Ministry of Communications via telegram, requesting an order to stop the company's assets from falling into the hands of foreigners. The mortgagees, unable to take over the docks, had the four foreign staff members who had been sent to report back to the foreigner who was holding the mortgage and the financial group. On one hand, they stopped paying the money, and on the other hand, they filed a complaint with the company. This matter has caused various disputes.

▲ Ling's Determination: Ling Jingshan, director of the Warehouse Affairs Section of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday, stating: "Shen Bao, I have refused to hand over the position, and various parties have criticized me, believing that I am reluctant to leave the position of Section Chief. I have already resigned from the position of Section Chief to Li Guojie and returned the letter of appointment from the manager of the China General Business Company in order to thank the people of the country. I am now going to Wuhan to take up the position of Chief Auditor at the Rural Financial Relief Office of Hubei and Anhui."

▲ Transfer Yesterday: On the afternoon of the 11th, Hong Dezhao, the deputy section chief of the China General Business Company, was sent to take over. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency inquired in the afternoon. According to a person in charge of the company, the transfer had been completed by the China General Business Company and would operate as usual from today.

▲ Renaming the Warehouse Section: The manager's office of the four warehouses of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (i.e., the Warehouse Affairs Section) located at No. 302 East Broadway Road was renamed the China General Business Company yesterday, and Hong Dezhao, the deputy section chief of the Warehouse Affairs Section of the company, was appointed by the company to continue in the position of director. The China General Business Company is fully responsible for all internal and external matters. There have been no changes to the internal personnel for the time being.

▲ Changing Opinions: After this incident occurred, it caused significant attention from all parties. A reporter from the Guowen News Agency interviewed a standing director of the company, whose nationalization had already been decided by the government, to inquire about his opinion. According to him, the government's decision to nationalize the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was originally to develop China's shipping industry. Today, this major incident has occurred at the company. Before we receive an appointment order, we cannot express anything, but the government must have a way to deal with this kind of illegal activity, etc.

▲ Appointment Order Will Be Issued: According to another director, the appointment orders for the supervisors and directors regarding the nationalization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be issued by the National Government within a few days. The government will handle the case of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's mortgage of the warehouses, etc.

▲ Employee Meeting: Upon hearing the news that the four docks had been mortgaged, all the employees of the five docks felt that mortgaging the four docks was tantamount to selling them off in disguise and that this small amount of Chinese shipping industry would be lost invisibly. The livelihoods of the employees of the five docks might be affected. At 5:00 PM yesterday, all the members of the union demanded that a general meeting be convened. The union then convened an emergency joint meeting of all the group leaders of the five docks. After the standing director of the union reported the truth of the matter, all the group leaders discussed how to respond. As a result, the following three measures were decided: (1) How should we respond to the mortgage of the docks, which affects the livelihoods and future of the employees? It was decided that opposing the mortgage should be the highest principle and guaranteeing livelihoods should be the minimum requirement. As for the method of action, the first step should be for all the group leaders to go to the company to petition, and the last resort should be a strike by all the members. (2) How should we express our opinion regarding the National Government's reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company? It was decided that a general meeting of all the members of the five docks should be convened at a set time to make a decision. (3) Regarding the issue of October's salary, it was decided to include a demand for its payment when the petition is submitted. The meeting was then adjourned, and it was planned that all the group leaders would go to the company to petition on Monday.

Zhu Hexiang Arrives in Shanghai 177

Will Go to Nanyang to Investigate Consulates

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, due to conflicting opinions between consulates in various parts of Nanyang and local overseas Chinese, and having repeatedly received documents accusing various consuls, has specially dispatched Zhu Hexiang, Director of the International Department, to conduct an investigation in order to rectify the situation. Zhu arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and is packing his luggage in preparation for departure.

▲ Motivation for Investigation: Overseas Chinese are most numerous in the various territories of Nanyang. In recent years, due to the global economic downturn, overseas Chinese merchants have felt the negative impact. At the same time, some unscrupulous elements among the consuls in various places have neglected their duty to protect overseas Chinese and have engaged in profit-seeking activities. The Ministry has received numerous cases accusing various consuls. Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wengan, in his indignation, ordered the dismissal and investigation of Su, the Consul General in San Francisco, and Liang, the Consul in Medan. On the one hand, Zhu Hexiang, Director of the International Department, was dispatched to Nanyang to conduct an investigation in order to engage in rectification and reform. At the same time, he will make every effort to find ways to alleviate the suffering of overseas Chinese.

▲ Place of Departure: After Zhu was ordered to go to Shanghai, the date of departure has not yet been determined, but it will not be too far off, roughly no later than the 20th of this month. Only Secretary Zhou Bofu will accompany him. All the procedures have been entrusted to the China Travel Service to handle. It is heard that Zhu will first go to Hong Kong to inspect Annam, then go through India, Singapore, Yangon, to Sumatra, Penang, Batavia, Calcutta, Medan, and then return to China via Siam. It is expected to take three and a half months. He will stay in each place for at least five days in order to fully accept the complaints of overseas Chinese and to inspect whether the consuls in each place are able to fulfill their duties. If there is sufficient time, he also intends to go to Manila.

▲ Consular Visa Matters: Since China implemented consular visa requirements for cargo manifests, the revenue situation has been quite good. According to the statistics for the first month, the total amount remitted to Beijing by consuls in various places was about 60,000 yuan. The amount collected by the customs was also 40,000 yuan, for a total of about 100,000 yuan. China has more than 80 consulates abroad. In Nanyang, there are about five in the Dutch colonies and four in the British colonies. Due to the delay in the commercial treaty with Vietnam, there has been no confirmation of the establishment of a consulate in French Annam, so there is no consulate there at this time. Regarding consular visas, except for Siam, where Chairman Zheng of the local Chinese Chamber of Commerce has been entrusted to act as an agent, it is also planned to contact Chairman Hong of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce in French Annam after Zhu arrives and entrust him to act as an agent.

▲ Rumors About the CER: Regarding rumors that Russia will transfer its rights over the Chinese Eastern Railway to France or Japan, it was heard yesterday that these rumors were completely propaganda created by the Japanese side. Although the Chinese Eastern Railway is nominally a joint Sino-Russian venture, the French also have a stake in it. This is because the railway was completed with French loans during the Tsarist era. After the Russian Revolution, the socialist Soviet government completely refused to acknowledge this loan, effectively defaulting on the debt. In 1907, after the Franco-Japanese Agreement was concluded, France recognized Japan's vested interests in Manchuria, and Japan also recognized France's vested interests in Yunnan and Guangxi, forming a secret collusion between France and Japan. Therefore, after the Northeast Incident, France and Japan still made proposals based on this agreement. However, France, in view of its recent position in Europe, has gradually felt threatened by Germany's demand for equal arms reduction. At the same time, the United States needed to court Britain and France on the Far East issue. As a result, France abandoned Japan and sided with the United States and Britain. Therefore, Japan's position in the Far East suddenly became isolated, and it had no choice but to send Matsuoka abroad to lobby and create rumors that Soviet Russia would transfer its rights over the Chinese Eastern Railway to France and Japan in order to deceive the world into believing that Russia and Japan were friendly. At the same time, it is proceeding with the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty with Soviet Russia, but Russia and Japan are fundamentally incompatible. Therefore, Matsuoka's trip to Russia will not be successful, etc.
