Editor's Remarks

Speaking Up for the Stars 233

— Han

Today, in the "Reader's Opinion" column, there is an article by Mr. Xi Zhan titled "Actors Must Go Among the People." I am publishing it not because his writing is particularly good or his opinions are insightful, but (no offense to Mr. Xi Zhan) because his thinking represents the impression of the general domestic film audience, or a large portion of it. He says, "Currently, most Chinese actors grow up in big cities, live in luxurious Western-style houses, wear gorgeous clothes, enjoy rich wine, and go everywhere in cars, all of which demonstrates a life under the glittering gold of capitalism." After reading this, I couldn't help but frown and smile. The smile and the frown both came because the same fantasy arose in my mind. It was as if I saw the gatherings of deities in Hollywood: reaching the magnificent mansions of Douglas Fairbanks and Mary Pickford, with many Rolls-Royces, Lincolns, Packards, Buicks, and silver-gray cars outside. Because the word "的" (de) after "cars" depicts the comings and goings of more than just one vehicle. Alas, what a wonderful rosy scene! Therefore, I closed my eyes and meditated on this, revealing a slight smile.

However, from the clouds, I tumbled down to the ground of the Suzhou Creek. What I actually see before my eyes in China is completely different from the fantasy of a few seconds ago. I recall that when the weather gets cold, actors with low incomes cannot afford new clothes and buy and wear used clothing on Wusong Road. They do sit in cars, but they are from the Yunfei Motor Company (unintentionally promoting Yunfei a bit). They are not luxurious, and four or five people ride in one, which is even more cost-effective than a rickshaw. Jin Yan is very popular, but he also has to wear second-hand clothes. Zhang Zhiyun rode in a car from the Lili Company (of course, promoting Yunfei, because she wouldn't agree not to promote Lili), and it even caused a bit of a stir. Chen Yumei advocates for simple clothing, perhaps because she cannot afford it, or at least because silk and satin are too expensive.

And then there is the hardship of the extras: freezing all night, starving for thirteen hours, and the reward for men is only one yuan, and for women, one yuan and twenty cents. This is also the life of an actor, but this kind of life is not even as good as pulling a rickshaw. But in the films, they have to pretend to be wealthy and grand. This leads to misunderstandings among the audience. This is what I want to speak up for on behalf of the stars, especially the poor ones.

In the end, with all industries in decline and livelihoods hanging by a thread, Western-style houses, cars, fancy clothes, and fine wine are what the stars pursue. But plums are sour and hang high on the tree. You can only look at them and swallow your saliva.

Overseas News

Zasu Pitts 234

— Wang Zhihong

The Female Charlie Chaplin of Hollywood

Charlie Chaplin is popular because his comedies are disguised tragedies; the most comical part is the scene that most evokes people's sympathy and deep thought. Eating a grand meal in The Gold Rush, the loss of a child in The Kid, and the ending of City Lights all prove the statement above.

Now, Hollywood people have found a female star who has the same style as Chaplin 丨丨Zasu Pitts丨丨 and they say that she is Chaplin's incarnation.

She was born in Kansas but grew up in Santa Cruz. In 1920, she married an actor, Tom Gallery. The first few years of their marriage were happy, but after seven years, they divorced! She was extremely unwilling to divorce, but the matter was beyond redemption, which left a huge scar on her heart.

She entered the film industry as early as 1917.

Unfortunately, she was ignored by Hollywood people for a long time. Later, she continued to play supporting roles in various films. With her dedicated research, her experience on the set, coupled with her inner refinement and the stimulation given by the environment, she created her current style and finally succeeded. Her performance can be seen in famous films like Monte Carlo; her comical interjections are also common in films starring Ann Harding and Constance Bennett.

Now, major directors feel that a film cannot have a good opening scene without her, so they often ask her to perform. With her performance, audiences smile with satisfaction as soon as they see her sorrowful face and her performance that transforms the sound of crying into something magical, comical but with a hint of sadness.

She is currently filming two full-length comedies, and after their release, the film industry will surely appreciate them.

— Morning Star

Films produced by the German Ufa company have long enjoyed a considerable reputation in China. However, since last year, due to the suspicions of the Japanese manager, Ufa products have disappeared from the Chinese film market. Now, the German Ufa headquarters has signed a long-term contract with the British-owned Wan Guo Film Company in Shanghai. Ufa films will again be screened in China and the Far East to meet the needs of the audience. The first film to be shown in China is Congress Dances. Looking at her graceful posture and alluring attire, who would be willing to hit her, especially her rosy cheeks? But she was ultimately slapped as many as nineteen times. Hearing this, you may be surprised and ask, "Who hit her?" She was hit by an Irishman named Pat O'Brien.

Reader's Opinion

"Actors Must Go Among the People" 239

— Xi Zhan

Looking at the recent articles in various newspapers about the direction that Chinese cinema should take in the future, most advocate that movies should be revolutionary and mass-oriented. Indeed, China is currently in a state of rapid turmoil, and serious national crises are before us. Movies that depict romantic love between men and women and shallow, comical movies are not needed. Undoubtedly, the general public has understood that movies are by no means for the enjoyment of a few idle people, nor are they the product of some surreal inspiration. Movies themselves are a form of serious social education and a powerful tool for promoting social progress.

However, most of the current Chinese actors grow up in big cities, live in luxurious Western-style houses, wear gorgeous clothes, enjoy rich wine, and go everywhere in cars, all of which demonstrates a life under the glittering gold of capitalism. Therefore, in this situation, even if there are excellent scripts depicting the suffering of oppressed villagers in rural areas, the cruelty of small businessmen being exploited by large capitalists, and the brutality of imperialism trampling on weak nations, the actors simply have not experienced or paid attention to the suffering of the oppressed. They often ruin a very valuable script, which is a pity. It is just like a poet who was born in the tropics. No matter how others explain to him the beauty and purity of winter snow, or even if he himself gathers materials about snow from various sources, he still cannot write good poems because he has never seen it with his own eyes. Similarly, in film art, if actors usually do not pay attention to the various expressions of proletarian life, even if the director explains it from many aspects during the performance, the effect is still like scratching an itch from outside one's boots. There is always a kind of distance, and of course, great and profound works cannot be produced under such circumstances.

Therefore, I hope that actors will often go among the people. Only in this way can they understand the lives of ordinary people and empathize with their hardships and difficulties, just like Mrs. Buck in America, because she had previously experienced rural life and was familiar with the psychological state of farmers, she was able to write novels that shocked the literary world. I hope that actors will often go among the people because only there can they find the object you want to study and enhance your art of expression.

Local News

Yang Naimei to Go to Hong Kong 240

— Mai

From This Point On, Leave the Silver Screen

Since Yang Naimei married Chen Xunmin, she has completely changed her previous romantic attitude. She is obedient and absolutely submissive to everything Chen desires. However, there is one thing she cannot obey, and that is "acting." Chen's original intention was that since she is now someone's wife, she should no longer reveal her beauty on the silver screen. However, Naimei had a prior agreement and had to fulfill her task, so she had to disobey Chen's orders. Although Chen was dissatisfied, he had to understand, so the feelings between the two did not deteriorate. However, Naimei did not want the feelings between the couple to change again, so her definite intention is that she will never pursue a career on the silver screen again.

Film Monographs

Believe in Yourself 241

— Chen Dabei

From this, we can know that from now on, all those who have already enjoyed the glory of stardom, if they do not constantly seek progress in the art of acting, their failure is certain. Because in the near future, there will definitely be a group of people who are more ambitious, more patient, and more courageous than them, who will show their talent on the screen, take their place, and replace them. By that time, the current group who rely solely on relatives and friends will naturally disappear.

Fellow art lovers! Please don't be afraid! "Success depends on human effort!" "Where there's a will, there's a way!" These are timeless truths! Summon your courage! Stand tall! March forward relentlessly on the road to stardom! Strive to give yourself a unique training! Resolve to create yourself into a future star! It all depends on whether you have the perseverance and determination to continue to work hard according to my unique learning methods, to practice continuously, and even after you succeed, you must continue to work hard!

Friend! Do you still have any doubts about my words of encouragement? Can't you believe in yourself? It doesn't matter! This is just your insatiable heart playing tricks. An insatiable heart is beneficial to you. People without this insatiable heart will become complacent. Complacency will limit your own progress.

Friend! I tell you! You must preserve your insatiable heart! But you must quickly burn away this part of your lack of confidence with the fire of perseverance! From today onwards, you must absolutely believe in yourself! You must believe that you have the ability to become a successful star!
